 After the dismissal of Finance Minister Haseeb Darabu in Jammu and Kashmir, the BJP and PDP coalition government are once again being questioned
 vitt mantri haseeb daraabu kii barkhaastagi ke baad bijepi alaakaman ne jammu-kashmir ke apane netaaon ko dilli talab kiya he
 If BJP sources are to be believed, Haseeb Darrabu, along with BJP General Secretary Ram Madhav, laid the foundation of BJP and PDP coalition government
 haseeb daraabu ne pichley hafte apane ek bayaan main kaha tha ki kashmir raajnneetik mudda nahin he, balki ye soshal mudda hai
 But the PDP always demands that Kashmir should be solved as a political problem and that it should solve the Kashmir problem only by negotiating with Pakistan
 isliye mukhyamantri mahabuuba kaa maananaa he ki haseeb daraabu kaa yah bayaan pidipi kii raajnneetik soch or party kii vichaardhaara ke khilaaf he
 The BJP was already hurt by the way the statements of Chief Minister Mehbooba Mufti or PDP leaders in the Major Aditya case or similar cases have come up in the past year about the encounter of terrorists
 ab haseeb daraabu kii barkhaastagi ne aag main ghi daalane kaa kaam kiya he
 That is why the state BJP leaders have been called to Delhi
 bijepi alaakaman ab pidipi ke saath gathbandhan main kya karnaa he isko lekar apane state ke netaaon ke saath aage kii ranneeti tay karegaa
 If sources are to be believed, the BJP high command is worried that Chief Minister Mehbooba Mufti has already started fearing elections
 isliye ab gathbandhan ke nunatam saajha kaarykram ke agenda ko chhodkar apane kor kattar muddon kii raajnneeti kii taraf aage badhane lagi he
 The BJP is considering all aspects of this alliance
 kyonki RSS pehle se is gathbandhan se kush nahin tha
 The Central Bureau of Investigation (CBI) has filed another charge sheet in the much-talked-about Vyapam scam in Madhya Pradesh
 PMT-2012 ghotaalaa maamle main sibiai kii ore se daakhil yachika main 592 logon ke naam shaamil hai
 The four Vyapam officers whose names have been included in it include the then Vyapam director Pankaj Trivedi, the then senior system analyst Nitin Mohindra, the then deputy system analyst Ajay Kumar Sen and the then programmer CK Mishra
 is chargeshit main 245 aropiyon ke naam pehali baar shaamil kiye gaye hai
 The CBI chargesheet also includes the names of 22 middlemen, 46 examiners, two medical college officials and two big racketeers
 iske alaava bhopal ke chaar privet collejon ke chairman ke naam bhi shaamil kiye gaye hai, jisamen chiraayu medical college ke chairman ajay goyanka, pipuls medical college ke chairman esen vijaywagia, medical college ke chairman suresh singh bhadauria, alen medical college ke chairman jeen chaukase shaamil hai
 At the same time, CBI has already given a clean chit to Madhya Pradesh Chief Minister Shivraj Singh Chauhan
 sibiai ne apni jaanch main congress netaa digvijay singh ke un aaropon ko khaarij kar diya tha, jisamen digvijay ne aarope lagaaya tha ki shivaraj singh chouhan ko bachaane ke liye hard discs se chhedchhad kii gai he

 An MP from Tamil Nadu's ruling party AIADMK has said that whoever talks about the health of Chief Minister Jayalalithaa, her tongue will be cut off
 namakkal se party saansad piaar sundaram ne vipakshi party diemke ke netaa em karunanidhi ke us bayaan par yah tippanee kii, jisamen karunanidhi ne kaha tha ki chunki jayalalita biimaar hai, isliye unhen pad chhod dena chahie
 Sundaram said, Karunanidhi wants Amma to rest
 aapaki umr kya he? vah 93 saal ke hai or kehete hai ki vah sau saal jeena chaahate hai
 He does not want to transfer power to his sons
 ek saansad ke rup main mujhe sanyamit rahanaa chahie, lekin agar koi krantikari netaa ammaa ke bare main kuch kahata he, to uski jubaan kaat lee jaaegi
 The comments is maheene kii shuruyaat main jayalalita kareeb 10 dinon tak kaam se dur raheen, jiske baad atakalon kaa bazaar garm ho gaya or vipakshi partiyon kii ore se kai tippaniyan saamne ain
 While the DMK has said that 67-year-old Jayalalithaa should step down as chief minister, Congress leader EVKS Ilangovan has demanded that the government should make it clear whether she (jayalalithaa) is unwell
 mukhyamantri jayalalita 15 july ko dobaaraa kaam par laut ain
 His party has denied reports that the chief minister is planning to go abroad for liver transplant and has called such reports a conspiracy to retaliate the opposition DMK
 jayalalita ne vidhansabha upachunaav main record maton se jeet darj karne ke baad 4 july ko vidhayak ke rup main shapath lee thi
 Party MP from Namakkal PR Sundaram made this comment on the statement by m Karunanidhi, leader of the opposition party DMK, in which Karunanidhi said that since Jayalalithaa is ill, she should step down
 sundaram ne kaha, karunanidhi chaahate hai ki ammaa ko aaraam karnaa chahie
 what is your age? He is 93 years old and says he wants to live a hundred years
 vah apane beton ko shakti hastantarit nahin karnaa chaahate hai
 As an MP i must remain restrained, but if a revolutionary leader says anything about Amma, her tongue will be cut off
 tippaniyan Earlier this month, Jayalalithaa was away from work for about 10 days, after which the speculation market started to heat up and several comments came from opposition parties
 ek ore jahaan diemke ne kaha he ki 67-varshiya jayalalita ko mukhyamantri kaa pad chhod dena chahie, vahiin congress netaa iwikees elangowan ne maang kii he ki sarkaar ko yah saaf karnaa chahie ki kya vah (jayalalita) aswasth hai
 Chief Minister Jayalalithaa returned to work on 15 July
 unki party ne in khabaron kaa khandan kiya he ki mukhyamantri liver transplant karaane ke liye videsh jane kaa kaarykram bana rahi hai or aisi khabaron ko vipakshi diemke kii badale kii sajeesh qaraar diya he
 Jayalalithaa was sworn in as an MLA on July 4 after winning by a record number of votes in the assembly by-election
 sundaram ne kaha, karunanidhi chaahate hai ki ammaa ko aaraam karnaa chahie

 zyada jaankara ke lieyaha clic karen Chanting of mantras has special significance in worshiping God
 devi-devataaon ko prasann karne ke liye mantron ke jaap kaa vidhaan he
 But people often use the same garland for chanting mantras
 jyotish ke jaankaron kii maane to har devi-devtaa kii aradhana ke liye ek vishesh maala tay he, jiske prayog se devtaa jaldi prasann hote hai

 aaie aapako bataate hai koun se dev mantra kaa jaap koun si maala se karnaa sahi hota he or ishwar kii upasana kaa mahatv kya he
 Importance of Mala in worship- There are many ways of praying, praying with words, kirtan or mantra - Mantras are considered to be most effective in these - Mantras converge immediately to the mind, their effect is also quick - Different effects in every mantra
 And there is different power- different garlands are used for chanting mantra- doing so gives full benefit of the power of different mantras- number in mantra chanting It is of special importance - Mala is also used to chant the right number of Mantras - the beads are attached to the beads in beads, usually there are 108 beads in the garland - sometimes there are 27 or 74 beads in the garland
 Precautions for use of Hammala- The number of beads of the rosary should be at least 27 or 108
 - har manake ke baad ek gaanth jarur lagi honi chahie
 - There should not be a touch of the garland with the index finger at the time of chanting the mantra - Sumeru should not be violated either
 - mantra jap ke samay maala kisi vastra se dhanki honi honi chahie yaa gomukhi main honi chahie
 - Before chanting the mantra, you should pray with a garland in your hand - Pray that chanting the mantra done with the garland should be successful
 - maala hameshaa vyaktigat honi chahie- duusare kii maala kaa prayog nahin karnaa chahie
 - The rosary with which you chant mantras should not be worn
 rudraksh kii maala kaa mahatv- saamanytah kisi bhi mantra kaa jaap rudraksh kii maala se kar sakate hai- shiv ji or unke parivaar ke liye mantra jaap rudraksh kii maala se laabhakaari hota he- mahamrityunjay or laghumrityunjay mantra keval rudraksh par hi japana chahiesphatik kii maala kaa mahatv- ye maala ekaagratha , sampannataa or shaanti kii maala maani jaati he- maan saraswati or maan lakshmi ke mantra is maala se japana uttam hota he- dhan prapti or ekaagratha ke liye sphatik kii maala dhaaran karenhaldi kii maala kaa mahatv- vishesh prayogon or manokamanaayon ke liye haldi kii maala kaa prayog kiya jaataa he- brihaspati dev or maan bagalaamukhi ke mantron ke liye haldi kii maala kaa prayog hota he- haldi kii maala se gyaan or santan prapti ke mantron kaa jaap bhi kar sakate henchndan kii maala kaa mahatv- chandan kii maala do prakaar kii hoti he - laal chandan or shwet chandan- devi ke mantron kaa jaap laal chandan kii maala se karnaa faldaayi hota he- bhagavan krishna ke mantron ke liye safed chandan kii maala kaa prayog kar sakate hantulsi kii maala kaa mahatv- vaishnav parampara main is maala kaa sarvaadhik mahatv he- bhagwaan vishnu or unke avtaron ke mantron kaa jaap isi maala se kiya jaataa he- ye maala dhaaran karne par vaishnav parampara kaa paalan jarur karnaa chahie- tulsi kii maala par kabhi bhi devi or shiv ji ke mantron kaa jap nahin karnaa chahie

 Nearly half of the companies interviewed said in a survey that they did not plan to make specific investments this year
 federation of indian chambers of commers and industry (fikki) or lekhapareekshan company price waterhousakupers (peedblusi) ne sanyukt taur par kiye gaye ek surveykshan (india manuphacch ring barometer) ke mutabik sust aarthik vikaas or utpaadan main giravat ke kaaran vinirmaan companiyaan phoonk-phoonk kar kadam rakh rahi hai

 tippaniyan 42 per cent of the companies want to provide additional facilities in their products, while 76 per cent of the companies are trying to reduce the price

 But it seems that companies are using this period to improve and prepare for the future
